fiscal year 2019. This net income tax charge is excluded from our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> results. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft
returned $8.5&nbsp;billion to shareholders in the form of share repurchases and dividends in the second quarter of fiscal year 2020. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;Strong execution from our sales teams and partners drove Commercial Cloud revenue to $12.5&nbsp;billion, up 39% year over year,&#148; said
Amy Hood, executive vice president and chief financial officer of Microsoft. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue in Productivity and Business Processes was
$11.8&nbsp;billion and increased 17% (up 19% in constant currency), with the following business highlights: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Every quarter Microsoft delivers hundreds of products, either as new releases, services, or enhancements to current products and services. These
releases are a result of significant research and development investments, made over multiple years, designed to help customers be more productive and secure and to deliver differentiated value across the cloud and the edge. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Here are the <U>major product releases and other highlights</U> for the quarter, organized by product categories, to help illustrate how we are
accelerating innovation across our businesses while expanding our market opportunities. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Environmental, Social, and Governance (ESG)
</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">To better execute on Microsoft&#146;s mission, we focus our Environmental, Social, and Governance (ESG) efforts where we can have
the most positive impact. To learn more about our latest initiatives and priorities, please visit our investor relations <U>ESG website</U>.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666"><B>Webcast Details </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Satya Nadella, chief executive officer, Amy Hood, executive vice president and chief financial
officer, Frank Brod, chief accounting officer, Keith Dolliver, deputy general counsel, and Michael Spencer, general manager of investor relations, will host a conference call and webcast at 2:30 p.m. Pacific time (5:30 p.m. Eastern time) today to
discuss details of the company&#146;s performance for the quarter and certain forward-looking information. The session may be accessed at <U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">http://www.microsoft.com/en-us/investor</FONT></U>. The webcast will be
available for replay through the close of business on January&nbsp;29, 2021. </FONT></P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Definition </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">We recorded a net charge of $157&nbsp;million during the three months ended December&nbsp;31, 2018 related to the TCJA. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">We have provided <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures related to the TCJA to aid investors in better understanding
our performance. We believe these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures assist investors by providing additional insight into our operational performance and help clarify trends affecting our business. For comparability of
reporting, management considers <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures in conjunction with GAAP financial results in evaluating business performance. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures
presented in this release should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Constant Currency </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft presents constant currency information to provide a framework for assessing how our underlying businesses performed excluding the effect
of foreign currency rate fluctuations. To present this information, current and comparative prior period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are converted into United States dollars using the average
exchange rates from the comparative period rather than the actual exchange rates in effect during the respective periods. All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year. Microsoft has provided this <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial information to aid investors in better understanding our performance. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented in this release should not be considered as
a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. </FONT></P>
</DIV></Center>
